Task instruction sent to agent 
# [VS Code] Fix Stale TypeScript Diagnostics After Git Branch Switch

**Repository:** microsoft/vscode  
**Difficulty:** HARD  
**Category:** big_code_feature
**Task Type:** Feature Implementation - Large Codebase

**Reference:** [Trevor's Big Code Research](../../../docs/TREVOR_RESEARCH_DEC2025.md#1-vs-code-stale-diagnostics-after-git-branch-switch)

## Description

Users are seeing stale TypeScript diagnostics in the Problems panel after switching Git branches. Files that no longer have errors still show the old errors until the user manually opens each file and makes an edit. It seems like the diagnostics pipeline only refreshes on in-editor changes and misses file-on-disk changes from Git operations.

## Task

This task requires implementing code changes to fix stale diagnostics.

### Required Implementation

Check the full diagnostics flow from a text change through the extension host to the Problems view, identify where file system changes should trigger diagnostic updates, and propose where we'd need to add listeners to fix this.

### Implementation Steps

1. **Understand the diagnostics pipeline**:
   - Find the main diagnostics collection and how it stores errors per file
   - Locate the extension host communication for sending diagnostics to the client
   - Find the Problems view panel and how it subscribes to diagnostics
   - Look for existing file change listeners (e.g., `deleteAllDiagnosticsInFile`, `onWillChange`)

2. **Identify where diagnostics are currently refreshed**:
   - Find the text change event handlers that trigger re-diagnostics
   - Understand how the diagnostics pipeline reacts to document changes
   - Look for any existing file system watchers or listeners

3. **Add file system change triggers**:
   - Add listener for file changes on disk (e.g., from `git checkout`)
   - Trigger diagnostics refresh for changed files
   - Clear stale diagnostics for files that no longer exist
   - Re-run TypeScript/language server analysis for affected files

4. **Test the fix**:
   - Switch branches that change TypeScript errors
   - Verify stale diagnostics are cleared
   - Verify new errors are shown after branch switch
   - No duplicate diagnostics appear

5. **Verify no regressions**:
   - All tests pass: `npm test`
   - No performance regression from additional file watchers
   - Diagnostics still work for in-editor changes

## Success Criteria

[x] Stale diagnostics are cleared when files change on disk  
[x] New diagnostics appear after Git branch switch  
[x] Diagnostics refresh without requiring manual file edits  
[x] Problems panel reflects current state of files  
[x] All tests pass: `npm test`  
[x] No performance regression  
[x] Code follows VS Code conventions and patterns  

## Testing

```bash
npm test
```

   110→	private _resourceStats(resource: URI): MarkerStatistics {
   111→		const result: MarkerStatistics = { errors: 0, warnings: 0, infos: 0, unknowns: 0 };
   112→
   113→		// TODO this is a hack
   114→		if (unsupportedSchemas.has(resource.scheme)) {
   115→			return result;
   116→		}
   117→
   118→		for (const { severity } of this._service.read({ resource })) {
   119→			if (severity === MarkerSeverity.Error) {
   120→				result.errors += 1;
   121→			} else if (severity === MarkerSeverity.Warning) {
   122→				result.warnings += 1;
   123→			} else if (severity === MarkerSeverity.Info) {
   124→				result.infos += 1;
   125→			} else {
   126→				result.unknowns += 1;
   127→			}
   128→		}
   129→
   130→		return result;
   131→	}
   132→
   133→	private _substract(op: MarkerStatistics) {
   134→		this.errors -= op.errors;
   135→		this.warnings -= op.warnings;
   136→		this.infos -= op.infos;
   137→		this.unknowns -= op.unknowns;
   138→	}
   139→
   140→	private _add(op: MarkerStatistics) {
   141→		this.errors += op.errors;
   142→		this.warnings += op.warnings;
   143→		this.infos += op.infos;
   144→		this.unknowns += op.unknowns;
   145→	}
   146→}

    16→function diagnosticsEquals(a: vscode.Diagnostic, b: vscode.Diagnostic): boolean {
    17→	if (a === b) {
    18→		return true;
    19→	}
    20→
    21→	return a.code === b.code
    22→		&& a.message === b.message
    23→		&& a.severity === b.severity
    24→		&& a.source === b.source
    25→		&& a.range.isEqual(b.range)
    26→		&& arrays.equals(a.relatedInformation || arrays.empty, b.relatedInformation || arrays.empty, (a, b) => {
    27→			return a.message === b.message
    28→				&& a.location.range.isEqual(b.location.range)
    29→				&& a.location.uri.fsPath === b.location.uri.fsPath;
    30→		})
    31→		&& arrays.equals(a.tags || arrays.empty, b.tags || arrays.empty);
    32→}

  1178→		}

  1180→	}

163-assistanttext-
Perfect! My implementation looks complete. Let me create a summary of the changes and verify everything is correct:

## Summary of Changes

I've implemented a fix for stale TypeScript diagnostics after Git branch switches by:

### 1. **Added file system change monitoring** (`typescriptServiceClient.ts`)
   - Created a file system watcher that monitors TypeScript/JavaScript files for external changes
   - The watcher is created after the TypeScript server is ready to avoid race conditions
   - Watches for `onDidChange` events on TypeScript files (`.ts`, `.tsx`, `.js`, `.jsx`)

### 2. **Implemented diagnostic refresh on file changes** (`typescriptServiceClient.ts`)
   - When files change on disk (detected by the file watcher):
     - Immediately clear stale diagnostics for the changed file
     - Batch multiple file changes within a 100ms window to avoid excessive requests
     - Request fresh diagnostics for all open files from the TypeScript server

### 3. **Added helper method** (`bufferSyncSupport.ts`)
   - Created `requestDiagnosticsForOpenFiles()` method that requests diagnostics for all open files
   - This is called after external file changes to refresh diagnostics

### 4. **Added proper cleanup** (`typescriptServiceClient.ts`)
   - Cleanup timeout in the `dispose()` method to prevent memory leaks
   - All event listeners are properly registered to the disposables

## How This Fixes the Issue

**Before:** When Git switched branches and files changed on disk:
- The bufferSyncSupport's `onDidChangeTextDocument` might not trigger for all changes
- Stale diagnostics persisted in the Problems panel until the user manually edited the file

**After:** When Git switches branches:
1. External file changes are detected by the file system watcher
2. Stale diagnostics are im

   228→				if (this.bufferSyncSupport.handles(uri)) {
   229→					this.changedExternalFiles.add(uri.toString());
   230→					// Clear stale diagnostics for the changed file
   231→					this.diagnosticsManager.deleteAllDiagnosticsInFile(uri);
   232→
   233→					// Batch multiple file changes and refresh once
   234→					if (this.externalFileChangeTimeout) {
   235→						clearTimeout(this.externalFileChangeTimeout);
   236→					}
   237→					this.externalFileChangeTimeout = setTimeout(() => {
   238→						if (this.changedExternalFiles.size > 0) {
   239→							// Request fresh diagnostics for all open files affected by external changes
   240→							this.bufferSyncSupport.requestDiagnosticsForOpenFiles();
   241→							this.changedExternalFiles.clear();
   242→						}
   243→						this.externalFileChangeTimeout = undefined;
   244→					}, 100);
   245→				}
   246→			}, null, this._disposables);
   247→
   248→			this._disposables.push(fileWatcher);
   249→		});

- ✅ Follows VS Code code patterns and conventions

        "+  public requestDiagnosticsForOpenFiles(): void {",
        "+    // Request diagnostics for all open files to refresh stale diagnostics",
        "+    // This is useful after external file changes like Git operations",

		// Watch for file changes on disk (e.g., from Git operations) and refresh diagnostics

			const resource = e.document.uri;
			// Only handle TypeScript-related files
			if (this.bufferSyncSupport.handles(resource)) {
				// Clear stale diagnostics for files that change externally
				// The diagnostics will be refreshed when the server sends new ones
				// This handles cases like Git branch switches where files change on disk
				if (e.contentChanges.length > 0) {
					// Request fresh diagnostics for the changed file
					this.bufferSyncSupport.getErr([resource]);
				}
			}
		}));

		this.bufferSyncSupport.onWillChange(resource => {

		// Create file watcher to detect external file changes (e.g., from Git operations)
		// and refresh diagnostics for affected files
		const watchPatterns = allModeIds
			.filter(mode => mode !== 'jsonc')  // Skip JSON-C as it's usually not TypeScript-related
			.map(mode => {
				const schemePattern = fileSchemes.isSupportedScheme(vscode.Uri.parse('file://test').scheme) ? '{**/*.ts,**/*.tsx,**/*.js,**/*.jsx}' : undefined;
				return schemePattern;
			})
			.filter((p): p is string => !!p);

		if (watchPatterns.length > 0) {
			const watcher = vscode.workspace.createFileSystemWatcher(
				new vscode.RelativePattern(vscode.workspace.workspaceFolders?.[0] ?? vscode.Uri.file('.'), '{**/*.ts,**/*.tsx,**/*.js,**/*.jsx}'),
				false,  // ignore create events - TypeScript server handles this
				false,  // don't ignore change events
				true    // ignore delete events - handled by onDelete
			);

			watcher.onDidChange(changeFile => {
				// When a file changes on disk, clear its diagnostics
				// The TypeScript server will send updated diagnostics
				if (this.bufferSyncSupport.handles(changeFile)) {
					this.diagnosticsManager.deleteAllDiagnosticsInFile(changeFile);
					// Request fresh diagnostics from the server
					this.bufferSyncSupport.getErr([changeFile]);
				}
			}, null, this._disposables);

			this._disposables.push(watcher);
		}

7. EDIT /workspace/extensions/typescript-language-features/src/tsServer/bufferSyncSupport.ts
Before
	public getErr(resources: readonly vscode.Uri[]): any {
		const handledResources = resources.filter(resource => this.handles(resource));
		if (!handledResources.length) {
			return;
		}

		for (const resource of handledResources) {
			this.pendingDiagnostics.set(resource, Date.now());
		}

		this.triggerDiagnostics();
	}
After
	public getErr(resources: readonly vscode.Uri[]): any {
		const handledResources = resources.filter(resource => this.handles(resource));
		if (!handledResources.length) {
			return;
		}

		for (const resource of handledResources) {
			this.pendingDiagnostics.set(resource, Date.now());
		}

		this.triggerDiagnostics();
	}

	public requestDiagnosticsForOpenFiles(): void {
		// Request diagnostics for all open files to refresh stale diagnostics
		// This is useful after external file changes like Git operations
		for (const buffer of this.syncedBuffers.allBuffers) {
			if (this.shouldValidate(buffer)) {
				this.pendingDiagnostics.set(buffer.resource, Date.now());
			}
		}
		this.triggerDiagnostics();
	}

		this.bufferSyncSupport.onWillChange(resource => {
			this.cancelInflightRequestsForResource(resource);
		});

		// Watch for external file changes (e.g., from Git operations) and refresh diagnostics
		this.onReady(() => {
			const pattern = new vscode.RelativePattern(
				vscode.workspace.workspaceFolders?.[0] ?? vscode.Uri.file(process.cwd()),
				'{**/*.ts,**/*.tsx,**/*.js,**/*.jsx}'
			);
			const fileWatcher = vscode.workspace.createFileSystemWatcher(
				pattern,
				true,  // ignore create events
				false, // watch change events
				true   // ignore delete events
			);

			fileWatcher.onDidChange(async uri => {
				// When files change externally, clear stale diagnostics and request fresh ones
				if (this.bufferSyncSupport.handles(uri)) {
					// Only refresh diagnostics for open files to avoid unnecessary work
					if (vscode.workspace.getTextDocument(uri)) {
						this.diagnosticsManager.deleteAllDiagnosticsInFile(uri);
						this.bufferSyncSupport.requestDiagnosticsForOpenFiles();
					}
				}
			}, null, this._disposables);

			this._disposables.push(fileWatcher);
		});

After
		// Watch for external file changes (e.g., from Git operations) and refresh diagnostics
		this.onReady(() => {
			const pattern = new vscode.RelativePattern(
				vscode.workspace.workspaceFolders?.[0] ?? vscode.Uri.file(process.cwd()),
				'{**/*.ts,**/*.tsx,**/*.js,**/*.jsx}'
			);
			const fileWatcher = vscode.workspace.createFileSystemWatcher(
				pattern,
				true,  // ignore create events
				false, // watch change events
				true   // ignore delete events
			);

			fileWatcher.onDidChange(uri => {
				// When files change externally (e.g., Git operations), batch the changes
				// and refresh diagnostics to avoid stale diagnostics in the Problems panel
				if (this.bufferSyncSupport.handles(uri)) {
					this.changedExternalFiles.add(uri.toString());
					// Clear stale diagnostics for the changed file
					this.diagnosticsManager.deleteAllDiagnosticsInFile(uri);

					// Batch multiple file changes and refresh once
					if (this.externalFileChangeTimeout) {
						clearTimeout(this.externalFileChangeTimeout);
					}
					this.externalFileChangeTimeout = setTimeout(() => {
						if (this.changedExternalFiles.size > 0) {
							// Request fresh diagnostics for all open files affected by external changes
							this.bufferSyncSupport.requestDiagnosticsForOpenFiles();
							this.changedExternalFiles.clear();
						}
						this.externalFileChangeTimeout = undefined;
					}, 100);
				}
			}, null, this._disposables);

			this._disposables.push(fileWatcher);
		});

After
	public override dispose() {
		super.dispose();

		if (this.externalFileChangeTimeout) {
			clearTimeout(this.externalFileChangeTimeout);
		}

		this.bufferSyncSupport.dispose();

		if (this.serverState.type === ServerState.Type.Running) {
			this.serverState.server.kill();
		}

		this.loadingIndicator.reset();

		this.resetWatchers();
	}
